breezy in Fedora 32

This page displays detailed information for a specific version of breezy. You might want go back to the main page of breezy.

Changelog

Date Author Change
2020-01-28 Fedora Release Engineering - 3.0.2-2 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_32_Mass_Rebuild
2019-12-01 Miro Hrončok - 3.0.2-1 - Update to 3.0.2
2019-10-24 Miro Hrončok - 3.0.1-4 - On Fedora 32+, replace bazaar with breezy https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Changes/ReplaceBazaarWithBreezy
2019-10-17 Miro Hrončok - 3.0.1-3 - Reenable all extension modules
2019-10-10 Miro Hrončok - 3.0.1-2 - Disable the _static_tuple_c extension module to workaround Python 3.8 problems (#1760260) - Other disabled modules depending on the above: _chk_map_pyx, _dirstate_helpers_pyx, _bencode_pyx, _btree_serializer_pyx
2019-09-04 Miro Hrončok - 3.0.1-1 - Package breezy
